Copy the method onto the manager.\n            new_methods[name] = create_method(name, method)\n        return new_methods\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_queryset(cls, queryset_class, class_name=None):\n        if class_name is None:\n            class_name = \"%sFrom%s\" % (cls.__name__, queryset_class.__name__)\n        return type(\n            class_name,\n            (cls,),\n            {\n                \"_queryset_class\": queryset_class,\n                **cls._get_queryset_methods(queryset_class),\n            },\n        )\n\n    def contribute_to_class(self, cls, name):\n        self.name = self.name or name\n        self.model = cls\n\n        setattr(cls, name, ManagerDescriptor(self))\n\n        cls._meta.add_manager(self)\n\n    def _set_creation_counter(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the creation counter value for this instance and increment the\n        class-level copy.\n        \"\"\"\n        self.creation_counter = BaseManager.creation_counter\n        BaseManager.creation_counter += 1\n\n    def db_manager(self, using=None, hints=None):\n        obj = copy.copy(self)\n        obj._db = using or self._db\n        obj._hints = hints or self._hints\n        return obj\n\n    @property\n    def db(self):\n        return self._db or router.db_for_read(self.model, **self._hints)\n\n    #######################\n    # Subclasses can override this method to\n        customize the behavior of the Manager.\n        \"\"\"\n        return self._queryset_class(model=self.model, using=self._db, hints=self._hints)\n\n    def all(self):\n        # We can't proxy this method through the `QuerySet` like we do for the\n        # rest of the `QuerySet` methods. Soft-delete using a queryset\n            count = Article.soft_objects.bulk_soft_delete(\n                Article.soft_objects.filter(published=False),\n                deleted_by=request.user\n            )\n\n            # Soft-delete using a list of IDs\n            count = Article.soft_objects.bulk_soft_delete([1, 2, 3])\n        \"\"\"\n        # Convert list of IDs to queryset if needed\n        if not isinstance(queryset_or_ids, QuerySet):\n            queryset = self.get_queryset().filter(pk__in=queryset_or_ids)\n        else:\n            queryset = queryset_or_ids\n\n        # Field doesn't exist, skip setting deleted_by\n                pass\n\n        # Execute bulk update using ORM operations\n        count = queryset.update(**update_data)\n\n        return count\n\n    def restore(\n        self,\n        queryset_or_ids: Union[QuerySet, Iterable[int]]\n    ) -> int:\n        \"\"\"\n        Restore soft-deleted records by unmarking them as deleted.\n\n        Performs a bulk update of soft-deleted records, setting is_deleted to False\n        and clearing the deletion timestamp and deleted_by information.\n\n        Args:\n            queryset_or_ids: Either a QuerySet object or an iterable of record IDs\n\n        Returns:\n            int: The count of records that were restored\n\n        Example:\n            # Restore using a queryset\n            count = Article.soft_objects.restore(\n                Article.soft_objects.filter(is_deleted=True, title__contains='Archive')\n            )\n\n            # Restore using a list of IDs\n            count = Article.soft_objects.restore([1, 2, 3])\n        \"\"\"\n        # Convert list of IDs to queryset if needed\n        if not isinstance(queryset_or_ids, QuerySet):\n            queryset = self.get_queryset().filter(pk__in=queryset_or_ids)\n        else:\n            queryset = queryset_or_ids\n\n        # Prepare update dictionary with ORM expressions\n        update_data = {\n            'is_deleted': False,\n            'deleted_at': None,\n        }\n\n        # Clear deleted_by if the model has that field\n        try:\n            self.model._meta.get_field('deleted_by')\n            update_data['deleted_by'] = None\n        except FieldDoesNotExist:\n            # Field doesn't exist, skip clearing deleted_by\n            pass\n\n        # Execute bulk update using ORM operations\n        count = queryset.update(**update_data)\n\n        return count\n\n\nclass ManagerDescriptor:\n    def __init__(self, manager):\n        self.manager = manager\n\n    def __get__(self, instance, cls=None):\n        if instance is not None:\n            raise AttributeError(\n                \"Manager isn't accessible via %s instances\" % cls.__name__\n            )\n\n        if cls._meta.abstract:\n            raise AttributeError(\n                \"Manager isn't available; %s is abstract\" % (cls._meta.object_name,)\n            )\n\n        if cls._meta.swapped:\n            raise AttributeError(\n                \"Manager isn't available; '%s' has been swapped for '%s'\"\n                % (\n                    cls._meta.label,\n                    cls._meta.swapped,\n                )\n            )\n\n        return cls._meta.managers_map[self.manager.name]\n\n\nclass EmptyManager(Manager):\n    def __init__(self, model):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.model = model\n\n    def get_queryset(self):\n        return super().get_queryset().none()\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":1,"oldLines":6,"newStart":1,"newLines":5,"lines":[" import copy"," import inspect","-from datetime import datetime"," from functools import wraps"," from importlib import import_module"," from typing import Iterable, Optional, Union"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}
